date: "2018-07-05"
categories: type-theory

---

This is my attempt to collect in just one-file, a basic overview of HoTT in Agda.
This source code was type-checked by Agda 2.5.4.

Based on:

<div class="references" markdown="1">
- https://github.com/HoTT/HoTT-Agda/
- https://mroman42.github.io/ctlc/agda-hott/Total.html
</div>

Agda has a pragma to work with HoTT (`--without-K`):

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="455" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="459" class="Keyword">OPTIONS</a> <a id="467" class="Option">--without-K</a> <a id="479" class="Symbol">#-}</a>
<a id="483" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="488" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="495" href="Agda.Primitive.html" class="Module">Agda.Primitive</a> <a id="510" class="Keyword">public</a>

<a id="518" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#518" class="Function">_</a> <a id="520" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="522" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="526" class="Comment">-- trick for avoiding Agda module errors (jekyll)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Universes
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type universe hierarchy. It hides Agda primitive
hierarchy and the keyword `Set`. It uses `Type` instead.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="799" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Universes"></a><a id="806" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#806" class="Module">Universes</a> <a id="816" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="825" class="Comment">-- Our Universe hierarchy. It is implemented over the primitive</a>
  <a id="891" class="Comment">-- Agda universe hierarchy but it uses Type instead of Set, the</a>
  <a id="957" class="Comment">-- usual name for the Universe in Agda.</a>

Types
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Empty Type

The empty type, representing falsehood.

<a id="1525" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="⊥"></a><a id="1530" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1530" class="Datatype">⊥</a> <a id="1532" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="1533" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1533" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="1535" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="1537" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1539" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="1544" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1533" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="1547" class="Keyword">where</a>

### Unit

The unit type is defined as record so that we also get the η-rule definitionally.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="1860" class="Comment">-- A record without fields is the unit type with a single</a>
<a id="1918" class="Comment">-- constructor.</a>
<a id="1934" class="Keyword">record</a> <a id="⊤"></a><a id="1941" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1941" class="Record">⊤</a> <a id="1943" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1945" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1097" class="Function">Type0</a> <a id="1951" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="1959" class="Keyword">constructor</a> <a id="⊤.★"></a><a id="1971" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1971" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a>

<a id="unit"></a><a id="1974" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1974" class="Function">unit</a> <a id="1979" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="1981" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1971" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a>

<a id="1984" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="1988" class="Keyword">BUILTIN</a> UNIT <a id="2001" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1941" class="Record">⊤</a> <a id="2003" class="Symbol">#-}</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Basic types of Martin-Löf type theory and some basic
functions.

### Σ-types

Sigma types are a particular case of records, but records can be
constructed using only sigma types. Note that l ⊔ q is the maximum
of two hierarchy levels l and q. This way, we define sigma types in
full generality, at each universe.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="2346" class="Keyword">infixr</a> <a id="2353" class="Number">60</a> <a id="2356" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2445" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a>
<a id="2360" class="Keyword">record</a> <a id="Σ"></a><a id="2367" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2367" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="2369" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2370" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2370" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="2373" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2373" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="2375" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="2377" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2378" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2378" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="2380" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2382" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="2387" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2370" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="2389" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="2391" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2391" class="Bound">T</a> <a id="2393" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2395" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2378" class="Bound">S</a> <a id="2397" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2399" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="2404" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2373" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="2406" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2408" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2410" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="2415" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2416" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2370" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="2419" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="2421" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2373" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="2423" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2425" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="2433" class="Keyword">constructor</a> <a id="Σ._,_"></a><a id="2445" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2445" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a>
  <a id="2451" class="Keyword">field</a>
    <a id="Σ.fst"></a><a id="2461" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2461" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="2465" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2467" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2378" class="Bound">S</a>

<a id="2485" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="2490" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2367" class="Module">Σ</a> <a id="2492" class="Keyword">public</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

### Products (×)

Product type as a particular case of the sigma

### Boolean

Boolean type, two constants true and false

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="3099" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Bool"></a><a id="3104" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3104" class="Datatype">Bool</a> <a id="3109" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3111" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1097" class="Function">Type0</a> <a id="3117" class="Keyword">where</a>

* Booleans can be defined by using a coproduct.

### Natural numbers

Natural numbers are the initial algebra for a constant and a
successor function. The BUILTIN declaration allows us to use
natural numbers in arabic notation.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="3407" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="ℕ"></a><a id="3412" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3412" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="3414" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3416" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1097" class="Function">Type0</a> <a id="3422" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="ℕ.zero"></a><a id="3430" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3430" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a> <a id="3435" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3437" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3412" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>
  <a id="ℕ.succ"></a><a id="3441" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3441" class="InductiveConstructor">succ</a> <a id="3446" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3448" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3412" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="3450" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3452" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3412" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>

<a id="Nat"></a><a id="3455" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3455" class="Function">Nat</a> <a id="3459" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3461" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3412" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>

<a id="3464" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="3468" class="Keyword">BUILTIN</a> NATURAL <a id="3484" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3412" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="3486" class="Symbol">#-}</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


### Common functions

#### Identity function
The identity function with implicit type.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="id"></a><a id="3603" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3603" class="Function">id</a> <a id="3606" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3608" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="3610" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3611" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3611" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="3612" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3614" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3615" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3615" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3617" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3619" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="3624" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3611" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="3625" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3627" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3629" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3615" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3631" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3633" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3615" class="Bound">A</a>

The identity function on a type `A` is `idf A`.

some errors for my jekyll configuration.

#### Instance Searh

### Identity Type

Equality is defined as an inductive type. Its induction principle
is the J-eliminator.

### PathOver

If you have a dependent type `B` over `A`, a path `p : x == y` in `A` and two
points `u : B x` and `v : B y`, there is a **type** `[u == v [ B ↓ p]]` of paths
from `u` to `v` lying over the path `p`.  By definition, if `p` is a constant
path, then `[u == v [ B ↓ p ]]` is just an ordinary path in the fiber.
[More info here](https://github.com/HoTT/HoTT-Agda/blob/master/core/lib/Base.agda#L115).

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="PathOver"></a><a id="6346" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6346" class="Function">PathOver</a> <a id="6355" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6357" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="6359" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6360" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6360" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="6363" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6363" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="6365" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6367" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6368" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6368" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="6370" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6372" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="6377" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6360" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="6379" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6381" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6382" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6382" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="6384" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6386" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6368" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="6388" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6390" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="6395" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6363" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="6397" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="6502" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="6508" class="Number">30</a> <a id="6511" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6346" class="Function">PathOver</a>
<a id="6520" class="Keyword">syntax</a> <a id="6527" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6346" class="Function">PathOver</a> B p u v <a id="6544" class="Symbol">=</a> u == v [ B ↓ p ]{% endraw %}</pre>

## Equational Reasoning

Equational reasoning is a way to write readable chains of equalities.
The idea is that you can write the following:

{% raw %}
```agda
  t : a == e
  t = a =⟨ p ⟩
      b =⟨ q ⟩
      c =⟨ r ⟩
      d =⟨ s ⟩
      e ∎
```
{% endraw %}

where `p` is a path from `a` to `b`, `q` is a path from `b` to `c`, and so on.
You often have to apply some equality in some context, for instance `p` could be
`ap ctx thm` where `thm` is the interesting theorem used to prove that `a` is
equal to `b`, and `ctx` is the context. [More info here](https://github.com/HoTT/HoTT-Agda/blob/master/core/lib/Base.agda#L270).

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="7218" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="EquationalReasoning"></a><a id="7225" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7225" class="Module">EquationalReasoning</a> <a id="7245" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7246" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7246" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="7248" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7250" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7251" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7251" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="7253" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7255" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="7260" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7246" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="7262" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7264" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="7273" class="Comment">-- Common combinators for equational reasoning. They allow us to</a>
  <a id="7340" class="Comment">-- write proof in an equational style. These versions have been</a>
  <a id="7406" class="Comment">-- adapted from the old version of the HoTT-agda library.</a>

<a id="7770" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="7775" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7225" class="Module">EquationalReasoning</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Actions on paths I

Properties and structure of the equality type.

### Equality

Types are higher groupoids.  If we see equalities as paths, this
is the inverse of a path. If we see equalities classically, this
is the symmetric property of equality.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="inv"></a><a id="8074" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8074" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="8078" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8080" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="8082" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8082" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="8083" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8085" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8086" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8086" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="8088" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8090" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="8095" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8082" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="8096" class="Symbol">}</a>  <a id="8099" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8100" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8100" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="8102" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8102" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="8104" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8106" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8086" class="Bound">A</a><a id="8107" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="8111" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8113" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8100" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="8115" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5183" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="8118" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8102" class="Bound">b</a>
  <a id="8122" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8124" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8102" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="8126" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5183" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="8129" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8100" class="Bound">a</a>
<a id="8131" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8074" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="8135" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8136" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5230" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="8141" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8141" class="Bound">a</a><a id="8142" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8144" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8146" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5230" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="8151" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8141" class="Bound">a</a>{% endraw %}</pre>
Functions are functors to equalities.  In other words, functions
preserve equalities.

## Properties on the groupoid

<a id="9849" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="9854" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8960" class="Module">·-Properties</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Transport

When we transport a proof of `(P a)` over an equality `(a == b)`, we
get a proof of `(P b)`.

                <a id="14226" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14228" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14229" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14229" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="14231" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14233" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14165" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14235" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5183" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="14238" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14167" class="Bound">y</a><a id="14239" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14241" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14243" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14244" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14244" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14246" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14248" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14175" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14250" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14165" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14252" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14254" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14193" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="14256" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14165" class="Bound">x</a><a id="14257" class="Symbol">)</a>

## Homotopy

In a type-theoretical sense, a homotopy between two
functions is a family of equalities between their applications.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="14714" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Homotopy"></a><a id="14721" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14721" class="Module">Homotopy</a> <a id="14730" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14731" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14731" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="14734" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14734" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="14736" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14738" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14739" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14739" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14741" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14743" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="14748" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14731" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="14750" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14752" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14753" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14753" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="14755" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14757" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14739" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14759" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14761" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="14766" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14734" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="14768" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14770" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="14778" class="Comment">-- A homotopy is a natural isomorphism between two functions, we will write</a>
  <a id="14856" class="Comment">-- f ∼ g when (f x == g x) for all x.</a>
  <a id="Homotopy.homotopy"></a><a id="14896" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14896" class="Function">homotopy</a> <a id="14905" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14907" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14908" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14908" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14910" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14910" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14912" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14914" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="14916" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14916" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14918" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14920" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14739" class="Bound">A</a><a id="14921" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14923" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14925" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14753" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="14927" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14916" class="Bound">x</a><a id="14928" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="14931" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14933" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="14938" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14939" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14731" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="14942" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="14944" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14734" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="14946" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="14950" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14896" class="Function">homotopy</a> <a id="14959" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14959" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14961" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14961" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14963" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14965" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14966" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14966" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14968" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14970" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14739" class="Bound">A</a><a id="14971" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14973" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14975" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14959" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14977" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14966" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14979" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5183" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="14982" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14961" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14984" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14966" class="Bound">x</a>

  <a id="Homotopy._∼_"></a><a id="14989" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14989" class="Function Operator">_∼_</a> <a id="14993" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14995" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14996" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14996" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14998" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14998" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="15000" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15002" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="15004" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15004" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="15006" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15008" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14739" class="Bound">A</a><a id="15009" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15011" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15013" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14753" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="15015" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15004" class="Bound">x</a><a id="15016" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="15019" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15021" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="15026" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15027" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14731" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="15030" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="15032" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14734" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="15034" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="15038" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15038" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="15040" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14989" class="Function Operator">∼</a> <a id="15042" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15042" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="15044" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15046" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14896" class="Function">homotopy</a> <a id="15055" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15038" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="15057" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15042" class="Bound">g</a>

  <a id="15062" class="Comment">-- Homotopy is an equivalence relation</a>
  <a id="Homotopy.h-refl"></a><a id="15103" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15103" class="Function">h-refl</a> <a id="15110" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15112" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15113" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15113" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="15115" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15117" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15118" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15118" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="15120" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15122" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14739" class="Bound">A</a><a id="15123" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15125" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15127" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14753" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="15129" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15118" class="Bound">x</a><a id="15130" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15132" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15134" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15113" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="15136" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14989" class="Function Operator">∼</a> <a id="15138" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15113" class="Bound">f</a>

<a id="15960" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="15965" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15527" class="Module">HomotopyComposition</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Naturality

Homotopy is natural, meaning that it satisfies the following
square commutative diagram.

A particular case of naturality on the identity function.

## Equivalence in HoTT

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="18246" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Equivalence"></a><a id="18253" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18253" class="Module">Equivalence</a> <a id="18265" class="Keyword">where</a>

    <a id="18351" class="Comment">-- Contractible maps. A map is contractible if the fiber in any</a>
    <a id="18419" class="Comment">-- point is contractible, that is, each element has a unique</a>
    <a id="18484" class="Comment">-- preimage.</a>
    <a id="Equivalence.DefinitionOfEquivalence.isContrMap"></a><a id="18501" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18501" class="Function">isContrMap</a> <a id="18512" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18514" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18515" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18515" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="18517" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18519" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18314" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="18521" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18523" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18328" class="Bound">B</a><a id="18524" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18526" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18528" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="18533" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18534" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18306" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="18537" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="18539" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18309" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="18541" class="Symbol">)</a>

    <a id="18595" class="Comment">-- There exists an equivalence between two types if there exists a</a>
    <a id="18666" class="Comment">-- contractible function between them.</a>

## Cartesian Product

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="22018" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="CartesianProduct"></a><a id="22025" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22025" class="Module">CartesianProduct</a> <a id="22042" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22043" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22043" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="22046" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22046" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="22048" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22050" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22051" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22051" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="22053" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22055" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="22060" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22043" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="22062" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22064" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22065" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22065" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="22067" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22069" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="22074" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22046" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="22076" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22078" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="22087" class="Comment">-- In a pair, the equality of the two components of the pairs is</a>
  <a id="22154" class="Comment">-- equivalent to equality of the two pairs.</a>
  <a id="CartesianProduct.prodComponentwise"></a><a id="22200" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22200" class="Function">prodComponentwise</a> <a id="22218" <a id="22932" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="22937" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22025" class="Module">CartesianProduct</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## DecidableEquality

A type has decidable equality if any two of its
elements are equal or different. This would be a particular
instance of the Law of Excluded Middle that holds even if we do not
assume Excluded Middle.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="23203" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="DecidableEquality"></a><a id="23210" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23210" class="Module">DecidableEquality</a> <a id="23228" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23229" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23229" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="23230" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23232" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="23241" class="Comment">-- A type has decidable equality if we can prove that any two of its</a>
  <a id="23312" class="Comment">-- elements are equal or different.</a>
  <a id="DecidableEquality.decEq"></a><a id="23350" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23350" class="Function">decEq</a> <a id="23356" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23358" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23359" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23359" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23361" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23363" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="23368" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23229" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="23369" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23371" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23373" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="23378" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23229" class="Bound">ℓ</a>
  <a id="23382" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23350" class="Function">decEq</a> <a id="23388" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23388" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23390" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23392" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23393" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23393" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="23395" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23395" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="23397" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23399" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23388" class="Bound">A</a><a id="23400" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23402" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23404" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23405" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23393" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="23407" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5183" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="23410" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23395" class="Bound">b</a><a id="23411" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23413" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2918" class="Datatype Operator">+</a> <a id="23415" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1692" class="Function">¬</a> <a id="23417" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23418" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23393" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="23420" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5183" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="23423" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23395" class="Bound">b</a><a id="23424" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="23429" class="Comment">-- The product of types with decidable equality is a type with</a>
  <a id="23494" class="Comment">-- decidable equality.</a>

<a id="23915" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="23920" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23210" class="Module">DecidableEquality</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Propositions

Propositions as described on the main text. A type
is a proposition if we can create a function making any two of its
elements equal. We create a type of propositions.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="24150" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Propositions"></a><a id="24157" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24157" class="Module">Propositions</a> <a id="24170" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="24179" class="Comment">-- A type is a mere proposition if any two inhabitants of the type</a>
  <a id="24248" class="Comment">-- are equal</a>
  <a id="Propositions.isProp"></a><a id="24263" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24263" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24270" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24272" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="24274" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24274" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24275" class="Symbol">}</a>  <a id="24278" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24279" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24279" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24281" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24283" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24288" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24274" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24289" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24291" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24293" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24298" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24274" class="Bound">ℓ</a>
  <a id="24302" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24263" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24309" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24309" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24311" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="24313" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="24315" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24315" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="24317" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24317" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="24319" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24321" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24309" class="Bound">A</a><a id="24322" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24324" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24326" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24315" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="24328" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5183" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="24331" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24317" class="Bound">y</a><a id="24332" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="24337" class="Comment">-- The type of mere propositions</a>
  <a id="Propositions.hProp"></a><a id="24372" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24372" class="Function">hProp</a> <a id="24378" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24380" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="24382" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24382" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24383" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24385" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24387" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24392" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24393" href="Agda.Primitive.html#627" class="Primitive">lsuc</a> <a id="24398" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24382" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24399" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="24403" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24372" class="Function">hProp</a> <a id="24409" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24410" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24410" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24411" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24413" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="24415" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2367" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="24417" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24418" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24423" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24410" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24424" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24426" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24263" class="Function">isProp</a>


  <a id="24437" class="Comment">-- The dependent function type to proposition types is itself a</a>
  <a id="24503" class="Comment">-- proposition.</a>
  <a id="Propositions.piProp"></a><a id="24521" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24521" class="Function">piProp</a> <a id="24528" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24530" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="24532" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24532" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="24535" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24535" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="24537" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24539" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24541" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24542" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24542" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24544" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24546" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24551" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24532" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="24553" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24555" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24557" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24558" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24558" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24560" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24562" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24542" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24564" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24566" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24571" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24535" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="24573" class="Symbol">}</a>
         <a id="24584" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24586" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="24588" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24588" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="24590" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24592" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24542" class="Bound">A</a><a id="24593" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24595" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24597" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24263" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24604" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24605" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24558" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24607" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24588" class="Bound">a</a><a id="24608" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="24611" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24613" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24263" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24620" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="24622" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24622" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="24624" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24626" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24542" class="Bound">A</a><a id="24627" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24629" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24631" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24558" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24633" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24622" class="Bound">a</a><a id="24634" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="24638" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24521" class="Function">piProp</a> <a id="24645" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24645" class="Bound">props</a> <a id="24651" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24651" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="24653" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24653" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="24655" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="24657" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20348" class="Function">funext</a> <a id="24664" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="24666" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24666" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="24668" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24670" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24645" class="Bound">props</a> <a id="24676" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24666" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="24678" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24679" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24651" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="24681" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24666" class="Bound">a</a><a id="24682" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24684" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24685" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24653" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="24687" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24666" class="Bound">a</a><a id="24688" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="24693" class="Comment">-- The product of propositions is itself a proposition.</a>
  <a id="Propositions.isProp-prod"></a><a id="24751" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24751" class="Function">isProp-prod</a> <a id="24763" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24765" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="24767" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24767" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="24770" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24770" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="24772" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24774" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24776" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24777" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24777" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24779" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24781" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24786" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24767" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="24788" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24790" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24792" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24793" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24793" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24795" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24797" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24802" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24770" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="24804" class="Symbol">}</a>
              <a id="24820" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24822" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24263" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24829" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24777" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24831" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24833" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24263" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24840" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24793" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24842" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24844" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24263" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24851" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24852" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24777" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24854" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2743" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="24856" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24793" class="Bound">B</a><a id="24857" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="24921" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="24926" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24157" class="Module">Propositions</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## Sets

Sets are types without any higher dimensional structure, all
parallel paths are homotopic and the homotopy is given by a
continuous function on the two paths.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="25134" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Sets"></a><a id="25141" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25141" class="Module">Sets</a> <a id="25146" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="25155" class="Comment">-- A type is a &quot;set&quot; by definition if any two equalities on the type</a>
  <a id="25226" class="Comment">-- are equal.</a>

<a id="25841" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="25846" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25141" class="Module">Sets</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## HLevels

Higher levels of the homotopical structure, where the
first levels are:

- Contractible types (0)
- Propositions (1)
- Sets (2)

They would correspond to homotopy levels. We only work with
these first levels.

## EquivalenceProp

Equivalence of two types is a proposition
Moreover, equivalences preserve propositions.

<a id="28109" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="28114" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#27327" class="Module">EquivalenceProp</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## Half-Adjoints

Half-adjoints are an auxiliary notion that helps us
to define a suitable notion of equivalence, meaning that it is a
proposition and that it captures the usual notion of equivalence.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="28358" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Halfadjoints"></a><a id="28365" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28365" class="Module">Halfadjoints</a> <a id="28378" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28379" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28379" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="28382" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28382" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="28384" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28386" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28387" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28387" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="28389" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28391" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="28396" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28379" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="28398" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28400" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28401" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28401" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="28403" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28405" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="28410" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28382" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="28412" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28414" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="28423" class="Comment">-- Half adjoint equivalence.</a>
  <a id="28454" class="Keyword">record</a> <a id="Halfadjoints.ishae"></a><a id="28461" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28461" class="Record">ishae</a> <a id="28467" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28468" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28468" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="28470" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28472" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28387" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="28474" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="28476" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28401" class="Bound">B</a><a id="28477" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28479" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28481" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="28486" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28487" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28379" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="28490" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="28492" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28382" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="28494" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28496" class="Keyword">where</a>

## Quasiinverses

Two functions are quasiinverses if we can construct
a function providing gfx = x and fgy = y for any given x and y.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="31215" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Quasiinverses"></a><a id="31222" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31222" class="Module">Quasiinverses</a> <a id="31236" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="31237" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31237" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="31240" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31240" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="31242" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="31244" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="31245" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31245" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="31247" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31249" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="31254" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31237" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="31256" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="31258" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="31259" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31259" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="31261" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31263" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="31268" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31240" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="31270" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="31272" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="33968" class="Comment">-- Half-adjoint equivalences are quasiinverses.</a>

     <a id="35432" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2461" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="35436" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="35437" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35045" class="Function">invEqv</a> <a id="35444" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35359" class="Bound">α</a><a id="35445" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="35447" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#4075" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="35449" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2461" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="35453" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35359" class="Bound">α</a>     <a id="35459" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7563" class="Function Operator">==⟨</a> <a id="35463" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20348" class="Function">funext</a> <a id="35470" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="35471" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#19617" class="Function">rlmap-inverse-h</a> <a id="35487" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35359" class="Bound">α</a><a id="35488" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="35490" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7563" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>
     <a id="35497" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3603" class="Function">id</a>
   <a id="35503" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7662" class="Function Operator">∎</a><a id="35504" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="35507" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="35512" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#34253" class="Module">EquivalenceComposition</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## Univalence

Voevodsky's univalence axiom is postulated. It induces
an equality between any two equivalent types. Some β and η rules
are provided.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="35711" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Univalence"></a><a id="35718" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35718" class="Module">Univalence</a> <a id="35729" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="35773" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="UnivalenceAxiom"></a><a id="35780" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35780" class="Module">UnivalenceAxiom</a> <a id="35796" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="35797" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35797" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="35798" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="35800" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="35801" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35801" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="35803" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35803" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="35805" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="35807" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#999" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="35812" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35797" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="35813" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="35815" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="36515" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="36520" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35780" class="Module">UnivalenceAxiom</a> <a id="36536" class="Keyword">public</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Somme lemmas about Univelance

{: .foldable}
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="36614" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="36617" class="Comment">--   module UnivalenceLemmas {ℓ} where</a>
<a id="36656" class="Comment">--     -- The identity equivalence creates the trivial path.</a>
<a id="36717" class="Comment">--     ua-id : {A : Type ℓ} → ua idEqv == refl A</a>
<a id="36766" class="Comment">--     ua-id {A} =</a>
<a id="36785" class="Comment">--       begin</a>
<a id="36800" class="Comment">--         ua idEqv              ==⟨ ap ua (sameEqv (refl id)) ⟩</a>
<a id="36865" class="Comment">--         ua (idtoeqv (refl A)) ==⟨ ua-η (refl A) ⟩</a>
<a id="36918" class="Comment">--         refl A</a>
<a id="36936" class="Comment">--       ∎</a>
<a id="36947" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="36950" class="Comment">--     -- The composition of equivalences is preserved into composition</a>
<a id="37022" class="Comment">--     -- of equalities.</a>
<a id="37047" class="Comment">--     ua-comp : {A B C : Type ℓ} → (α : A ≃ B) → (β : B ≃ C) → ua (compEqv α β) == ua α · ua β</a>
<a id="37143" class="Comment">--     ua-comp α β =</a>
<a id="37164" class="Comment">--       begin</a>
<a id="37179" class="Comment">--         ua (compEqv α β)                               ==⟨ ap (λ x → ua (compEqv x β)) (inv (ua-β α)) ⟩</a>
<a id="37286" class="Comment">--         ua (compEqv (idtoeqv (ua α)) β)                ==⟨ ap (λ x → ua (compEqv (idtoeqv (ua α)) x))</a>
<a id="37391" class="Comment">--                                                            (inv (ua-β β)) ⟩</a>
<a id="37470" class="Comment">--         ua (compEqv (idtoeqv (ua α)) (idtoeqv (ua β))) ==⟨ ap ua lemma ⟩</a>
<a id="37546" class="Comment">--         ua (idtoeqv (ua α · ua β))                     ==⟨ ua-η (ua α · ua β) ⟩</a>
<a id="37629" class="Comment">--         ua α · ua β</a>
<a id="37652" class="Comment">--       ∎</a>
<a id="37663" class="Comment">--       where</a>
<a id="37678" class="Comment">--         lemma : compEqv (idtoeqv (ua α)) (idtoeqv (ua β)) == idtoeqv (ua α · ua β)</a>
<a id="37764" class="Comment">--         lemma = sameEqv (</a>
<a id="37793" class="Comment">--           begin</a>
<a id="37812" class="Comment">--             fst (idtoeqv (ua β)) ∘ fst (idtoeqv (ua α))                 ==⟨ refl _ ⟩</a>
<a id="37900" class="Comment">--             (transport (λ x → x) (ua β)) ∘ (transport (λ x → x) (ua α)) ==⟨ transport-comp (ua α) (ua β) ⟩</a>
<a id="38010" class="Comment">--             transport (λ x → x) (ua α · ua β)                           ==⟨ refl _ ⟩</a>
<a id="38098" class="Comment">--             fst (idtoeqv (ua α · ua β))</a>
<a id="38141" class="Comment">--           ∎)</a>
<a id="38157" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="38160" class="Comment">--     -- Inverses are preserved.</a>
<a id="38194" class="Comment">--     ua-inv-r : {A B : Type ℓ} → (α : A ≃ B) → ua α · ua (invEqv α) == refl A</a>
<a id="38274" class="Comment">--     ua-inv-r α =</a>
<a id="38294" class="Comment">--       begin</a>
<a id="38309" class="Comment">--         ua α · ua (invEqv α)      ==⟨ inv (ua-comp α (invEqv α)) ⟩</a>
<a id="38379" class="Comment">--         ua (compEqv α (invEqv α)) ==⟨ ap ua (compEqv-inv α) ⟩</a>
<a id="38444" class="Comment">--         ua idEqv                  ==⟨ ua-id ⟩</a>
<a id="38493" class="Comment">--         refl _</a>
<a id="38511" class="Comment">--       ∎</a>

<a id="38525" class="Comment">--     ua-inv : {A B : Type ℓ} → (α : A ≃ B) → ua (invEqv α) == inv (ua α)</a>
